Actor CatacombApocalypse_CyberMage : CatacombTrilogy_EnemyBase
{
	Health 120
	Speed 15
	+FLOAT
	+NOGRAVITY
	+NOBLOOD
	+DROPOFF

	DamageFactor "ElectricBolt", 2.0

Actor Catacomb_CybermageBall : Catacomb_MagicMissileProjectile
{
	Damage(7)
	SeeSound "Catacomb/MMisFire"
	DamageType "Plasma"
	Speed 20
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			CT21 IJ 4 BRIGHT
			Loop
		Death:
			TNT1 A 5
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}	

Actor CatacombApocalypse_InvisibleHorror : CatacombTrilogy_EnemyBase
{
	Health 200
	Radius 25
	Height 56
	Speed 20
	-COUNTKILL

	Tag "Invisible Horror"
	Obituary "Our savior %o has fallen to an Invisible Horror."
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)

		Spawn2:		
			TNT1 A 2 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			TNT1 AAAAAAA 4 A_Chase
			Loop
		Melee:

			CT22 C 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(15, "Catacomb/XTerm", "Catacomb/XTerm", "CatacombDamage", true)
			Goto See
		Pain:	
			CT22 D 2
			CT22 D 2 A_Pain
			Goto Melee
		Death:
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			CT22 D 10 A_Scream
			CT22 E 10 A_NoBlocking
			CT22 F -1 
			Stop	
		Pain.MightyBoot:

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_MantaRay_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_MantaRay_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_MantaRay_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 2
			TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Death.ExpanderDMG:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			CT26 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			CT26 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop				
	}
}				

actor CatacombApocalypse_MantaRay_Shrink : CatacombApocalypse_MantaRay

	+NOTRIGGER

	MaxDropOffHeight 0

	Height 16

	Speed 1

			CT26 F 10

			CT26 A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT26 A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)

Actor CatacombApocalypse_CyberPox : CatacombTrilogy_EnemyBase
{
	Health 250
	Radius 32
	Height 64
	Speed 10
	BloodColor "fc fc fc"
	Tag "Cyber Pox"
	+DONTRIP
	DamageFactor "MarathonFusion", 2.0
	DamageFactor "Tesla", 2.0
	DamageFactor "ElectricBolt", 2.0
	DamageFactor "PoisonBolt", 0		
	Obituary "Our savior %o has fallen to a Cyber Pox."
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			CT27 A 0
			CT27 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			CT27 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NoHeadshots",1)
			CT27 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			CT27 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:			
			CT27 AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			CT27 AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			CT27 F 8 A_FaceTarget
			CT27 G 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("Catacomb_CyberPoxBall",40,8,0,8)
			CT27 G 8 Bright A_CustomMissile("Catacomb_CyberPoxBall",40,-8,0,8)
			Goto See
		Pain:
			CT27 E 2
			CT27 E 2 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Death:
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			CT27 H 5 BRIGHT A_Scream
			CT27 I 5 BRIGHT A_NoBlocking
			CT27 HIHI 5 BRIGHT
			CT27 J 0 BRIGHT A_PlaySound("Catacomb/BigExplosion", CHAN_BODY)
			CT27 J 5 A_Explode(120, 120, 1, false)
			CT27 K -1  A_KillMaster
			Stop
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			CT27 E 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
			CT27 E 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MarathonStun:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NothingSpeed")
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("marathon/tech50/stun","body",0,0)
			CT27 E 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Gravity
			CT27 E 30 A_Pain
			CT27 E 70
			Goto See		
		Pain.LifeLeech:

			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			CT27 A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster
			Stop				
	}
}

Actor CatacombApocalypse_Spectre : CatacombTrilogy_EnemyBase
{
	Health 150
	Speed 15
	Radius 30
	Height 48
	PainChance 48
	-SOLID
	-SHOOTABLE
	+NOPAIN
	+NORADIUSDMG
	Tag "Oil Monster"
	BloodColor "39 39 39"
	DeathSound "Catacomb/BigExplosion"
	Obituary "Our savior %o has fallen to an Oil Monster."
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			CT29 A 0
			CT29 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
			CT29 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			CT29 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		Spawn2:		
			CT29 AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			CT29 AAABBB 4 A_Chase
			CT29 A 0 A_Jump(56, "Rise")
			CT29 AAABBB 4 A_Chase
			Loop
		Rise:
			CT29 C 8 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN, 0)
			CT29 C 0 A_ChangeFlag(NORADIUSDMG, 0)
			CT29 D 8 A_SetSolid
			CT29 E 8 A_SetShootable
			Goto UpLoop
		UpLoop:
			CT29 E 0 A_Jump(48, "Shot")
			CT29 EEFF 4 A_Chase
			CT29 E 0 A_Jump(8, "Sink")
			CT29 EEFF 4 A_Chase
			CT29 E 0 A_Jump(48, "Shot")
			CT29 EEFF 4 A_Chase
			CT29 E 0 A_Jump(8, "Sink")
			CT29 EEFF 4 A_Chase
			CT29 E 0 A_Jump(48, "Shot")
			Loop
		Sink:
			CT29 E 8 A_UnsetShootable
			CT29 D 8 A_UnsetSolid
			CT29 C 8 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN, 1)
			Goto See
		Shot:
			CT29 D 0 A_FaceTarget
			CT29 E 8 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("Catacomb_SmogProjectile", 32,0,0)
			Goto See
		Pain:
			CT29 F 2
			CT29 F 2 A_Pain
			Goto UpLoop
		Death:
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			CT29 G 15 A_Scream
			CT29 H 15 A_NoBlocking
			CT29 I 15
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)

			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
			CT29 F 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MarathonStun:

			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("marathon/tech50/stun","body",0,0)

			TNT1 A 0 A_Gravity
			CT29 F 30 A_Pain
			CT29 F 70
			Goto See

			Goto Pain

			TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster

			stop
		Death.CalebFire:
		Death.LifeLeech:

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop				
	}

actor CatacombApocalypse_Spectre_Shrink : CatacombApocalypse_Spectre
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE

	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN

	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1

		SpawnLoop:

			Loop
		See:

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT29 F 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT29 F 2 A_Chase("","")	
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_Spectre", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)

			Stop			
		}
}

		See:

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_GoldTroll_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_GoldTroll_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 2
			TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Death.ExpanderDMG:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			CT05 L 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			CT05 L 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop				
	}
}				

actor CatacombApocalypse_GoldTroll_Shrink : CatacombApocalypse_GoldTroll
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			CT05 P 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			CT05 L 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 L 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 L 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 M 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 M 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 N 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 N 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 O 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CT05 O 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CatacombApocalypse_GoldTroll", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

		Death.Nuke:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID", 0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Scream

			"####" "#################" 3 A_Fadeout(0.05)
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			stop			
	}
}
